# Historical Yamato/Japanese characters 1000008700-1000009899
# First unused index: 1000009800

# Swap from Yamato to Japanese around 800-850 (for the Imperial Family, it would be the children of Junna and Ninmyo), but let people alive at that point remain Yamato since it is a parent culture and thus not a cause for rebellion

##### The Imperial Family

# People before Emperor Keitai have been skipped
# All of these should have the amaterasu_descendant trait
# Includes people that later founded Minamoto/Taira/Tachibana branches, but not their descendants

### Emperor Keitai (1000008700) and his children (that have at least one verifiable date)

1000008700 = {
	name = "Ohodo" # Emperor Keitai
	dynasty = 1000027000 # Imperial Family
	religion = shinto
	culture = yamato
	trait = amaterasu_descendant
	450.1.1 = {
		birth = yes
	}
	# Married Princess Tashiraka (born 489), daughter of Emperor Ninken
	# Consorts:
	# - Owari Menokohime,daughter of Owari Kusaka)
	# - Mio Wakakohime,younger sister of Mio Tsunoori)
	# - Hirohime, daughter of Prince Sakata
	# - Okinaga Omino, daughter of Okinaga Mate
	# - Manda Sekihime, daughter of Manda Omochi
	# - Mio Yamatohime, daughter of Mio Katahi
	# - Wani Haehime, daughter of Wani Kawachi
	# - Hirohime, daughter of Ne
	507.3.3 = {
		name = "Keitai"
	}
	531.3.10 = {
		death = yes
	}
}

		birth = yes
	}
	# Married Princess Kasuga Yamada, daughter of Emperor Ninken
	# Consorts:
	# - Kose Satehime (daughter of Kose Ohito)
	# - Kose Kakarihime (daughter of Kose Ohito)
	# - Yakahime (daughter of Mononobe Itabi)
	531.3.10 = {
		name = "Ankan"
	}
	536.1.25 = {
		death = yes
	}
}

1000008703 = {

		birth = yes

		add_spouse = 1000008704 # Before 538
	}
	# Consorts:
	# - Princess Wayakahime, daughter of Emperor Senka
	538.1.1 = {
		add_consort = 1000008705 # Before 539
	}
	# - Princess Hikage, daughter of Emperor Senka
	# - Soga Kitashihime, daughter of Soga Iname
	# - Soga Oane, daughter of Soga Iname
	# - Kasuga Nukano, daughter of Kasuga Hifuri
	539.12.5 = {
		name = "Kinmei"
	}
	571.4.15 = {
		death = yes
	}
}

	# - Princess Nukatabe, daughter of Emperor Kinmei
	569.1.1 = {
		add_consort = 1000008710 # Before 570
	}
	# - Kasuga Ominako, daughter of Kasuga Nakakimi
	# - Unako Otoshi, daughter of Ohoka no Obito no Okuma
	571.4.30 = {
		name = "Bidatsu"

		death = yes
	}
}

		}
	}

	826.1.1 = {
		add_spouse = 1000009625 # Date unknown, but they had a son in 827
	}
	# Consorts:
	# - Fujiwara Sawako, daughter of Fujiwara Fusatsugu

		add_consort = 1000009507 # Unknown; they had a child in 828
	}
	# - Fujiwara Sadako, daughter of Fujiwara Mimori
	835.1.1 = {
		add_consort = 1000009400 # Unclear date, but they had a child in 836
	}
	# - Shigeno Tsunako, daughter of Shigeno Sadanushi
	# - Tachibana Kageko, daughter of Tachibana Ujikimi
	# - Fujiwara Musuko
	# - Kii Taneko, daughter of Kii Natora
	# - A woman from the Mikuni clan
	# - Fujiwara Katoko, daughter of Fujiwara Fukutomaro
	# - Fujiwara Warawako, daughter of Fujiwara Michito
	# - Princess Takamune, daughter of Prince Okaya
	# - A woman from the Yamaguchi clan

			set_character_flag = emperor_ninmyo_used # If deposed, don't reuse the name!

	name = "Kuniharu" # Emperor Go-Nijo
	dynasty = 1000027000 # Imperial Family
	religion = shinto
	culture = japanese
	trait = amaterasu_descendant
	father = 1000009231 # Emperor Go-Uda
	# Mother was Horikawa/Minamoto Motoko
	trait = child_of_consort
	1285.3.9 = {
		birth = yes
		effect = {
			set_character_flag = emperor_nijo
		}
	}
	1301.3.2 = {
		name = "Nijo"
		add_trait = under_regency
		effect = {
			set_character_flag = emperor_nijo_used # If deposed, don't reuse the name!
		}
	}
	# Married Fujiwara Kinshi, daughter of Tokudaiji Kintaka
	# Consorts:
	# - Fujiwara Tamako, daughter of Ichijo Sanetsune
	# - Fujiwara Muneko, daughter of Itsutsuji Munechika
	# - Koto Naishi, daughter of Taira Munetoshi
	# - Dainagon-no-Tsubone, daughter of Sanjo Kinyasu
	# - "Lady Mikushige", daughter of Sanjo Kinchika
	# - Daughter of Taira Nobusuke
	# - Shindainagon-no-Tsubone
	1308.9.10 = {
		death = yes
	}
}

1000009243 = {
	name = "Takaharu" # Emperor Go-Daigo
	dynasty = 1000027000 # Imperial Family
	religion = shinto
	culture = japanese
	trait = amaterasu_descendant
	father = 1000009231 # Emperor Go-Uda
	# Mother was Itsutsuji/Fujiwara Chushi
	trait = child_of_consort
	trait = ambitious # Successfully overthrew the Kamakura Shogunate
	trait = flamboyant_schemer # His plans got discovered in 1324
	trait = trusting # His plans were betrayed in 1331
	trait = just # Sought to reform the legal system
	trait = proud # Wanted to become an absolute ruler
	trait = lustful # Had a ton of children
	trait = hedonist
	1288.11.26 = {
		birth = yes
		effect = {
			set_character_flag = emperor_daigo
		}
	}
	1318.4.30 = {
		name = "Daigo"
		add_trait = under_regency
		effect = {
			set_character_flag = emperor_daigo_used # If deposed, don't reuse the name!
		}
	}
	# Married Saionji Kishi, daughter of Saionji Sanekane
	# Married Princess Junshi, daughter of Emperor Go-Fushimi
	1334.1.13 = {
		add_spouse = 1000009255
	}
	# Consorts:
	# - Fujiwara Eishi, daughter of Nijo Michihira
	# - Fujiwara Chikako, daughter of Itsutsuji Munechika
	# - Dainagon'nosuke, daughter of Kitabatake Moroshige
	# - Shin-Ansatsu-tenji, daughter of Jimyoin Yasufuji
	# - Sochi-no-suke
	# - Koto no Naishi, daughter of Saionji Tsunafusa
	# - Shosho no Naishi, daughter of Sugawara Arinaka
	# - Fujiwara/Ano Renshi, daughter of Ano Kinkado
	# - Minamoto Chikako, daughter of Kitabatake Morochika
	# - Fujiwara Tameko, daughter of Nijo Tameyo
	# - Fujiwara Jisshi, daughter of Toin Saneo
	# - Fujiwara Moriko, daughter of Toin Saneyasu
	# - Princess Kenshi, daughter of Emperor Kameyama
	1322.1.1 = {
		add_consort = 1000009289 # Date unknown; they had a son in 1323
	}
	# - Fujiwara/Nijo Michiko, daughter of Nijo Tamemichi
	# - Ichijo no Tsubone, daughter of Saionji Sanetoshi
	# - Shonagon no Naishi, daughter of Shijo Takasuke
	# - Dainagon-no-Tsubone, daughter of Ogimachi Saneakira
	# - Saemon-no-kami-no-tsubone, daughter of Nijo Tametada
	# - Gon-no-Chunagon no Tsubone, daughter of Sanjo Kinyasu
	# - Daughter of Yoshida Sadafusa
	# - Bomon-no-Tsubone, daughter of Bomon Kiyotada
	# - Daughter of Horikawa Mototomo
	# - Minamoto Yasuko, daughter of Minamoto Yasutoki
	# - Wakamizu-no-Tsubone, daughter of Minamoto Yasutoki
	# - Daughter of Horiguchi Sadayoshi
	# - Konoe no Tsubone
	1333.5.18 = {
		remove_trait = under_regency
	}
	1336.2.25 = {
		add_trait = under_regency
	}
	1339.9.19 = {
		death = yes
	}
}
